    <TR>
        <TD>
            <p ALIGN="LEFT">
            Below are the official entrants for the 2016 Lottery (December 5, 2015).
            The Ticket Count refers to the fact that lottery applicants receive additional chances
            in the drawing for each consecutive failure to gain entry in a prior year at 2^(n-1) where n is the number of consecutive years entering the lottery.
            </p>
            <p>
            Please report any corrections to <a href="mailto:lottery@wser.org">lottery@wser.org</a> before December 1. After December 1 the ticket counts are assumed to be correct.
            </p>

            <P ALIGN="LEFT"><B>These are final ticket counts.</B>
            <P>&nbsp;</P>
